(00:00) a complete guide to candlestick pattern trading understanding candlestick patterns goes far beyond just memorizing certain formations it is a method to read a price chart right now we're looking at raw data pure and naked price action if we strip everything off the chart and this is the most important information for trader that tells you everything you need to know about the intentions of all other market participants what the buyers and sellers are thinking who is in control and what is the future direction of the market by understanding what the candlesticks are
(00:31) telling you you can get better understanding of price movement we can identify where on the chart is increase in buying pressure or selling pressure if there is indecision in the market or how strong the momentum is or if there's exhaustion of certain price movement every small price change matters nothing is random in price session and therefore knowing what to look for on each candle is paramount to achieve consistent profitability candlesticks are representation of price movement they basically depict the tug of war between
